f(t,A)= -0.1286242133\,\sqrt{A}\;-\;0.1286242133\,A\,e^{-0.0593843782\,t}\;+\;0.3894244877\,\sin(0.5829315814\,A)
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **exactly** the sum of:
1) a \(\sqrt{A}\) term with coefficient \(-0.1286...\) (no shifts, no abs/max unless they reduce identically to \(\sqrt{A}\) on the whole domain),
2) an \(A e^{kt}\) term with coefficient \(-0.1286...\) and \(k=-0.05938...\),
3) a pure \(\sin(\omega A)\) term with amplitude \(0.3894...\) and **no phase shift**,
and **no extra terms** (no constants, no extra \(A\), rational, log, etc.), unless their coefficients can be set to 0.

Also note: candidates using \(\sqrt{\max(0,A)}\) or \(|A|^{0.5}\) cannot equal \(\sqrt{A}\) for all real \(A\). Since the task requires equality “for all values of the feature variables”, those forms only match if GT had the same piecewise definition (it doesn’t). So any candidate whose only square-root-like term is \(\sqrt{\max(0,A)}\) or \(|A|^{0.5}\) cannot match GT globally.
